She motioned to draw a rather old looking, blunt, and well-used Kunai from the confines of her sleeve. It wasn&#39;t much to look at, but it had a purpose and she was about to show it. 

A moment more and she kicked up a flat rock from the ground before she caught it, and then motioned towards the gathered bundle of sticks before she rolled the rock forward, and then followed with the Kunai. 

A brief strike, and she smeared it across the stone-face before a few sparks flickered forth.
